<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>A search reveals that the original, published 1887, was for piano duet. Piano solo versions are arrangements.  The first 7 pieces are in C major (not A major for no.1) (the 6th is a scherzo, the 7th a march), etc.- is this quite the same set despite the same name and opus number? Odd.
</p>
